3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.

2.1.1 Tastatur (2 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive input has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<input action="/sok" class="w-auto w-10/12 h-10 px-8 text-sm bg-gray-700 border-2 border-white border-opacity-50 rounded-lg lg:w-11/12 pr-22 focus:outline-none" method="get" name="s" placeholder="Søk"
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive button has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<button aria-label="Søk" class="absolute top-0 mt-5 mr-5 left-2" tabindex="-1" type="submit"> <svg class="w-5 h-5 text-white fill-current" height="512px" id="Capa_1" style="enable-background:new 0 0 5

MODERATE
